# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes API Server Admission Webhook Chain

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement the API server admission webhook chain: the webhook admission controller, the webhook call dispatch, and the admission response aggregation.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the domain domain.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

Perfect! I've successfully completed the analysis. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Summary: Kubernetes API Server Admission Webhook Chain

I've identified **15 Go source files** that implement the API server admission webhook chain in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository. These files are organized in a clear flow:

### Key Files Found:

1. **Webhook Configuration Management** (2 files):
   - Mutating and validating webhook configuration managers that load webhook definitions from the cluster

2. **Admission Controller Entry Points** (2 files):
   - MutatingAdmissionWebhook plugin
   - ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugin

3. **Generic Webhook Infrastructure** (2 files):
   - Core Webhook controller with dispatch logic
   - Dispatcher and Source interfaces

4. **Webhook Call Dispatchers** (2 files):
   - Mutating dispatcher (sequential calls)
   - Validating dispatcher (parallel calls with error aggregation)

5. **Request/Response Handling** (1 file):
   - AdmissionReview creation and response verification

6. **Webhook Configuration & Communication** (4 files):
   - Webhook accessors and configuration types
   - REST client manager for webhook calls
   - Error handling types
   - Status error conversion

### Key Design Patterns:

- **Sequential vs. Parallel**: Mutating webhooks are called sequentially, while validating webhooks run in parallel using goroutines
- **Error Aggregation**: Validating webhooks collect all errors and return the first one (logs others)
- **Failure Policies**: Both support "Fail" (reject) or "Ignore" (continue on webhook failure)
- **Dynamic Configuration**: Webhook configurations are watched and cached, allowing runtime updates without restart
- **Audit Integration**: Both webhook types emit audit annotations and warnings

Handles errors and continues or fails based on failure policy\\n\\n### Validating Webhooks (Parallel)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- validatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Pre-filters webhooks first, then spawns goroutines for parallel execution\\n- Pre-filtering phase:\\n  1. Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\nThe core webhook controller is implemented in:\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**: Webhook struct that coordinates the entire flow\\n  - NewWebhook(): Factory function that creates webhook with client manager, namespace/object matchers, and dispatcher\\n  - Dispatch(): Called by both mutating and validating plugins, checks exemptions, gets webhook list from hookSource, delegates to dispatcher\\n  - ShouldCallHook(): Determines if a webhook should be invoked by checking namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions\\n\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go**: Defines interfaces\\n  - Dispatcher interface: Defines Dispatch(ctx, attr, o, hooks) error contract\\n  - Source interface: Returns list of webhooks and readiness status\\n  - WebhookInvocation struct: Describes how to call a specific webhook\\n\\n## 3. Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook invocation with different concurrency models:\\n\\n### Mutating Webhooks (Sequential)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Iterates through webhooks sequentially\\n- For each webhook:\\n  1. Calls callAttrMutatingHook() which:\\n     - Validates dry-run constraints\\n     - Calls CreateAdmissionObjects() to create AdmissionReview request\\n     - Gets REST client from ClientManager\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Applies JSON patches to object if provided\\n     - Handles failures with failure policy (Fail or Ignore)\\n  3. Updates audit annotations from webhook response\\n  4. Handles errors and continues or fails based on failure policy\\n\\n### Validating Webhooks (Parallel)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- validatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Pre-filters webhooks first, then spawns goroutines for parallel execution\\n- Pre-filtering phase:\\n  1. Checks all webhooks against rules and selectors\\n  2. Caches versioned attributes for each matching webhook\\n- Parallel execution phase:\\n  1. Uses sync.WaitGroup to run each webhook call in a goroutine\\n  2. Each goroutine calls callHook() which:\\n     - Creates AdmissionReview request via CreateAdmissionObjects()\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook via REST client\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Collects errors in errCh channel\\n  3. Webhook Communication Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/client.go**:\\n- ClientManager: Manages REST clients for webhook calls\\n  - Caches clients to avoid duplicate creation\\n  - Handles authentication via kubeconfig\\n  - Resolves webhook service URLs\\n  - Manages TLS certificates\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/error.go**:\\n- Error types for webhook communication failures\\n- ErrCallingWebhook: Wraps webhook call failures\\n- ErrWebhookRejection: Wraps webhook rejection responses\\n\\n## Request Flow Summary\\n\\nMutating flow: Admit() \u2192 Dispatch() \u2192 ShouldCallHook() \u2192 mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch() \u2192 callAttrMutatingHook() \u2192 REST client \u2192 VerifyAdmissionResponse() \u2192 apply patches\\n\\nValidating flow: Validate() \u2192 Dispatch() \u2192 ShouldCallHook() (pre-filter) \u2192 validatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (spawn goroutines) \u2192 callHook() (parallel) \u2192 REST client \u2192 VerifyAdmissionResponse() \u2192 aggregate errors\\n\\nThe chain implements proper error handling with failure policies (Fail/Ignore), audit annotation collection, warning propagation, and support for dry-run requests.\"\n}\n",

Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook invocation with different concurrency models:\\n\\n### Mutating Webhooks (Sequential)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Iterates through webhooks sequentially\\n- For each webhook:\\n  1. Updates audit annotations from webhook response\\n  4. Checks all webhooks against rules and selectors\\n  2. Caches versioned attributes for each matching webhook\\n- Parallel execution phase:\\n  1. \"The Kubernetes API server admission webhook chain consists of three main phases:\\n\\n## 1. Webhook Admission Controller Entry Points\\n\\nTwo admission plugins serve as the entry points:\\n- **MutatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go): Plugin struct implementing admission.MutationInterface, with Admit() method that delegates to Webhook.Dispatch()\\n- **ValidatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go): Plugin struct implementing admission.ValidationInterface, with Validate() method that delegates to Webhook.Dispatch()\\n\\n## 2. Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\nThe core webhook controller is implemented in:\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**: Webhook struct that coordinates the entire flow\\n  - NewWebhook(): Factory function that creates webhook with client manager, namespace/object matchers, and dispatcher\\n  - Dispatch(): Called by both mutating and validating plugins, checks exemptions, gets webhook list from hookSource, delegates to dispatcher\\n  - ShouldCallHook(): Determines if a webhook should be invoked by checking namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions\\n\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go**: Defines interfaces\\n  - Dispatcher interface: Defines Dispatch(ctx, attr, o, hooks) error contract\\n  - Source interface: Returns list of webhooks and readiness status\\n  - WebhookInvocation struct: Describes how to call a specific webhook\\n\\n## 3. Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook invocation with different concurrency models:\\n\\n### Mutating Webhooks (Sequential)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Iterates through webhooks sequentially\\n- For each webhook:\\n  1. Calls ShouldCallHook() to check if webhook applies\\n  2. Calls callAttrMutatingHook() which:\\n     - Validates dry-run constraints\\n     - Calls CreateAdmissionObjects() to create AdmissionReview request\\n     - Gets REST client from ClientManager\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Applies JSON patches to object if provided\\n     - Handles failures with failure policy (Fail or Ignore)\\n  3. Updates audit annotations from webhook response\\n  4. Handles errors and continues or fails based on failure policy\\n\\n### Validating Webhooks (Parallel)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- validatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Pre-filters webhooks first, then spawns goroutines for parallel execution\\n- Pre-filtering phase:\\n  1. Checks all webhooks against rules and selectors\\n  2. Caches versioned attributes for each matching webhook\\n- Parallel execution phase:\\n  1. Uses sync.WaitGroup to run each webhook call in a goroutine\\n  2. Each goroutine calls callHook() which:\\n     - Creates AdmissionReview request via CreateAdmissionObjects()\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook via REST client\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Collects errors in errCh channel\\n  3. Aggregates all errors: if multiple failures, returns first error (logs others)\\n  4. Handles panics in webhook calls with deferred panic recovery\\n\\n## 4. Request/Response Handling\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go**:\\n- CreateAdmissionObjects(): Creates AdmissionReview request and response objects\\n  - Generates unique request UID\\n  - Creates versioned AdmissionReview in webhook's preferred version (v1 or v1beta1)\\n  - Returns request object and response object for decoding\\n- VerifyAdmissionResponse(): Validates and extracts webhook response\\n  - Verifies UID matches request\\n  - For mutating: validates patch and patchType are provided together\\n  - For validating: ensures no patch is returned\\n  - Extracts audit annotations, warnings, and mutation status\\n  - Returns AdmissionResponse struct with Allowed, Patch, Result fields\\n\\n## 5. Webhook Communication Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/client.go**:\\n- ClientManager: Manages REST clients for webhook calls\\n  - Caches clients to avoid duplicate creation\\n  - Handles authentication via kubeconfig\\n  - Resolves webhook service URLs\\n  - Manages TLS certificates\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/error.go**:\\n- Error types for webhook communication failures\\n- ErrCallingWebhook: Wraps webhook call failures\\n- ErrWebhookRejection: Wraps webhook rejection responses\\n\\n## Request Flow Summary\\n\\nMutating flow: Admit() \u2192 Dispatch() \u2192 ShouldCallHook() \u2192 mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch() \u2192 callAttrMutatingHook() \u2192 REST client \u2192 VerifyAdmissionResponse() \u2192 apply patches\\n\\nValidating flow: Validate() \u2192 Dispatch() \u2192 ShouldCallHook() (pre-filter) \u2192 validatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (spawn goroutines) \u2192 callHook() (parallel) \u2192 REST client \u2192 VerifyAdmissionResponse() \u2192 aggregate errors\\n\\nThe chain implements proper error handling with failure policies (Fail/Ignore), audit annotation collection, warning propagation, and support for dry-run requests.\"\n}\n",

\"The Kubernetes API server admission webhook chain consists of three main phases:\\n\\n## 1. Webhook Admission Controller Entry Points\\n\\nTwo admission plugins serve as the entry points:\\n- **MutatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go): Plugin struct implementing admission.MutationInterface, with Admit() method that delegates to Webhook.Dispatch()\\n- **ValidatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go): Plugin struct implementing admission.ValidationInterface, with Validate() method that delegates to Webhook.Dispatch()\\n\\n## 2. Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\nThe core webhook controller is implemented in:\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**: Webhook struct that coordinates the entire flow\\n  - NewWebhook(): Factory function that creates webhook with client manager, namespace/object matchers, and dispatcher\\n  - Dispatch(): Called by both mutating and validating plugins, checks exemptions, gets webhook list from hookSource, delegates to dispatcher\\n  - ShouldCallHook(): Determines if a webhook should be invoked by checking namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions\\n\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go**: Defines interfaces\\n  - Dispatcher interface: Defines Dispatch(ctx, attr, o, hooks) error contract\\n  - Source interface: Returns list of webhooks and readiness status\\n  - WebhookInvocation struct: Describes how to call a specific webhook\\n\\n## 3. Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook invocation with different concurrency models:\\n\\n### Mutating Webhooks (Sequential)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Iterates through webhooks sequentially\\n- For each webhook:\\n  1. Calls ShouldCallHook() to check if webhook applies\\n  2. Calls callAttrMutatingHook() which:\\n     - Validates dry-run constraints\\n     - Calls CreateAdmissionObjects() to create AdmissionReview request\\n     - Gets REST client from ClientManager\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Applies JSON patches to object if provided\\n     - Handles failures with failure policy (Fail or Ignore)\\n  3. Updates audit annotations from webhook response\\n  4. Handles errors and continues or fails based on failure policy\\n\\n### Validating Webhooks (Parallel)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- validatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Pre-filters webhooks first, then spawns goroutines for parallel execution\\n- Pre-filtering phase:\\n  1. Checks all webhooks against rules and selectors\\n  2. Caches versioned attributes for each matching webhook\\n- Parallel execution phase:\\n  1. Uses sync.WaitGroup to run each webhook call in a goroutine\\n  2. Each goroutine calls callHook() which:\\n     - Creates AdmissionReview request via CreateAdmissionObjects()\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook via REST client\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Collects errors in errCh channel\\n  3. Aggregates all errors: if multiple failures, returns first error (logs others)\\n  4. Handles panics in webhook calls with deferred panic recovery\\n\\n## 4. Request/Response Handling\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go**:\\n- CreateAdmissionObjects(): Creates AdmissionReview request and response objects\\n  - Generates unique request UID\\n  - Creates versioned AdmissionReview in webhook's preferred version (v1 or v1beta1)\\n  - Returns request object and response object for decoding\\n- VerifyAdmissionResponse(): Validates and extracts webhook response\\n  - Verifies UID matches request\\n  - For mutating: validates patch and patchType are provided together\\n  - For validating: ensures no patch is returned\\n  - Extracts audit annotations, warnings, and mutation status\\n  - Returns AdmissionResponse struct with Allowed, Patch, Result fields\\n\\n## 5. Webhook Communication Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/client.go**:\\n- ClientManager: Manages REST clients for webhook calls\\n  - Caches clients to avoid duplicate creation\\n  - Handles authentication via kubeconfig\\n  - Resolves webhook service URLs\\n  - Manages TLS certificates\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/error.go**:\\n- Error types for webhook communication failures\\n- ErrCallingWebhook: Wraps webhook call failures\\n- ErrWebhookRejection: Wraps webhook rejection responses\\n\\n## Request Flow Summary\\n\\nMutating flow: Admit() \u2192 Dispatch() \u2192 ShouldCallHook() \u2192 mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch() \u2192 callAttrMutatingHook() \u2192 REST client \u2192 VerifyAdmissionResponse() \u2192 apply patches\\n\\nValidating flow: Validate() \u2192 Dispatch() \u2192 ShouldCallHook() (pre-filter) \u2192 validatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (spawn goroutines) \u2192 callHook() (parallel) \u2192 REST client \u2192 VerifyAdmissionResponse() \u2192 aggregate errors\\n\\nThe chain implements proper error handling with failure policies (Fail/Ignore), audit annotation collection, warning propagation, and support for dry-run requests.\"\n}\n",

Generic Webhook Infrastructure\\n\\nThe core webhook controller is implemented in:\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**: Webhook struct that coordinates the entire flow\\n  - NewWebhook(): Factory function that creates webhook with client manager, namespace/object matchers, and dispatcher\\n  - Dispatch(): Called by both mutating and validating plugins, checks exemptions, gets webhook list from hookSource, delegates to dispatcher\\n  - ShouldCallHook(): Determines if a webhook should be invoked by checking namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions\\n\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go**: Defines interfaces\\n  - Dispatcher interface: Defines Dispatch(ctx, attr, o, hooks) error contract\\n  - Source interface: Returns list of webhooks and readiness status\\n  - WebhookInvocation struct: Describes how to call a specific webhook\\n\\n## 3. Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook invocation with different concurrency models:\\n\\n### Mutating Webhooks (Sequential)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Iterates through webhooks sequentially\\n- For each webhook:\\n  1. Calls ShouldCallHook() to check if webhook applies\\n  2. Calls callAttrMutatingHook() which:\\n     - Validates dry-run constraints\\n     - Calls CreateAdmissionObjects() to create AdmissionReview request\\n     - Gets REST client from ClientManager\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Applies JSON patches to object if provided\\n     - Handles failures with failure policy (Fail or Ignore)\\n  3. Updates audit annotations from webhook response\\n  4. Handles errors and continues or fails based on failure policy\\n\\n### Validating Webhooks (Parallel)\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go**:\\n- validatingDispatcher.Dispatch(): Pre-filters webhooks first, then spawns goroutines for parallel execution\\n- Pre-filtering phase:\\n  1. Checks all webhooks against rules and selectors\\n  2. Caches versioned attributes for each matching webhook\\n- Parallel execution phase:\\n  1. Uses sync.WaitGroup to run each webhook call in a goroutine\\n  2. Each goroutine calls callHook() which:\\n     - Creates AdmissionReview request via CreateAdmissionObjects()\\n     - Makes POST request to webhook via REST client\\n     - Verifies response with VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n     - Collects errors in errCh channel\\n  3. Aggregates all errors: if multiple failures, returns first error (logs others)\\n  4. Handles panics in webhook calls with deferred panic recovery\\n\\n## 4. Request/Response Handling\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go**:\\n- CreateAdmissionObjects(): Creates AdmissionReview request and response objects\\n  - Generates unique request UID\\n  - Creates versioned AdmissionReview in webhook's preferred version (v1 or v1beta1)\\n  - Returns request object and response object for decoding\\n- VerifyAdmissionResponse(): Validates and extracts webhook response\\n  - Verifies UID matches request\\n  - For mutating: validates patch and patchType are provided together\\n  - For validating: ensures no patch is returned\\n  - Extracts audit annotations, warnings, and mutation status\\n  - Returns AdmissionResponse struct with Allowed, Patch, Result fields\\n\\n## 5. Webhook Communication Infrastructure\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/client.go**:\\n- ClientManager: Manages REST clients for webhook calls\\n  - Caches clients to avoid duplicate creation\\n  - Handles authentication via kubeconfig\\n  - Resolves webhook service URLs\\n  - Manages TLS certificates\\n\\n**staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/error.go**:\\n- Error types for webhook communication failures\\n- ErrCallingWebhook: Wraps webhook call failures\\n- ErrWebhookRejection: Wraps webhook rejection responses\\n\\n## Request Flow Summary\\n\\nMutating flow: Admit() \u2192 Dispatch() \u2192 ShouldCallHook() \u2192 mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch() \u2192 callAttrMutatingHook() \u2192 REST client \u2192 VerifyAdmissionResponse() \u2192 apply patches\\n\\nValidating flow: Validate() \u2192 Dispatch() \u2192 ShouldCallHook() (pre-filter) \u2192 validatingDispatcher.Dispatch() (spawn goroutines) \u2192 callHook() (parallel) \u2192 REST client \u2192 VerifyAdmissionResponse() \u2192 aggregate errors\\n\\nThe chain implements proper error handling with failure policies (Fail/Ignore), audit annotation collection, warning propagation, and support for dry-run requests.\"",

4. EDIT /workspace/answer.json
Before
## 2. Generic Webhook Infrastructure

The core webhook controller is implemented in:
- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**: Webhook struct that coordinates the entire flow
  - NewWebhook(): Factory function that creates webhook with client manager, namespace/object matchers, and dispatcher
  - Dispatch(): Called by both mutating and validating plugins, checks exemptions, gets webhook list from hookSource, delegates to dispatcher
  - ShouldCallHook(): Determines if a webhook should be invoked by checking namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions

- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go**: Defines interfaces
  - Dispatcher interface: Defines Dispatch(ctx, attr, o, hooks) error contract
  - Source interface: Returns list of webhooks and readiness status
  - WebhookInvocation struct: Describes how to call a specific webhook
After
## 2. Webhook Configuration Management

Two configuration managers load webhook configurations from the Kubernetes cluster:
- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go**:
  - mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager: Implements Source interface, fetches MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects via informer
  - Watches for changes to webhook configurations in real-time
  - Caches and returns list of active mutating webhooks

- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go**:
  - validatingWebhookConfigurationManager: Implements Source interface, fetches ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects via informer
  - Watches for changes to webhook configurations in real-time
  - Caches and returns list of active validating webhooks

## 3. Generic Webhook Infrastructure

The core webhook controller is implemented in:
- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go**: Webhook struct that coordinates the entire flow
  - NewWebhook(): Factory function that creates webhook with client manager, namespace/object matchers, and dispatcher
  - Dispatch(): Called by both mutating and validating plugins, checks exemptions, gets webhook list from hookSource, delegates to dispatcher
  - ShouldCallHook(): Determines if a webhook should be invoked by checking namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions

- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go**: Defines interfaces
  - Dispatcher interface: Defines Dispatch(ctx, attr, o, hooks) error contract
  - Source interface: Returns list of webhooks and readiness status
  - WebhookInvocation struct: Describes how to call a specific webhook
